====Rules===

[D6] [Your Dice Roll Is tile Movement]

[hit  = 1-2] [Graze = 3-4] [5 = neutral] [ 6 = miss]

[hit = - 2 tiles] 

[Graze = -1 tile]

[Neutral = 0 tile interferance]

[Miss = + 1 tile]

=================

Experimental Rule:

landing on a space below the mushroom means you can move to the space above it.</font></font></font>

He removed silky fabrics before walking out to the male area with a towel and shorts on. The reticent young boy slipped into the water, placing a palm onto the sand used for decoration. He would start practicing imbuing it with his Chakra.

After accomplishing that, he would shift it around without weaving a single seal.
